Immediately discontinue use and contact your physician if any adverse reactions occur. Keep out of reach of children. Exposure to moisture or heat may cause powder to clump or harden. &lt;button class="accordion2"&gt;Warning&lt;/button&gt;
&lt;div class="panel" style="text-align: left;"&gt;
&lt;strong&gt;Warnings:&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt; Contains 274 mg of caffeine per serving or about as much caffeine as two and a half cups of coffee. Avoid using with other caffeinated products or if you are sensitive to caffeine because too much caffeine may cause nervousness, irritability, sleeplessness and occasionally, rapid heartbeat. Consult your physician prior to using this product if you are pregnant, nursing, under 18 years of age, taking medication or have a medical condition. Immediately discontinue use and contact your physician if any adverse reactions occur. Keep out of reach of children. Exposure to moisture or heat may cause powder to clump or harden. Store in a cool, dry place away from direct sunlight, humidity and high temperatures. Replace lid securely after each use. This product contains a silica gel pack. Do Not Eat. Contents may settle during shipping. Sold by weight, not volume.&lt;/div&gt;

Antioxidants are thought to scavenge naturally occurring but unwanted particles in the body known as free radicals. Consult your physician prior to using this product if you are pregnant, nursing, under 18 years of age, taking medication, have a medical condition or sensitive to caffeine. Store in a cool, dry place, avoid direct sunlight, humidity and high temperatures. Replace lid securely after each use. This product contains a silica gel pack. Do Not Eat. For non-training days consume one serving upon rising in morning and one serving mid-day between meals.&lt;/div&gt;

Store in a cool, dry place, avoid direct sunlight, humidity and high temperatures. Replace lid securely after each use. This product contains a silica gel pack. Do not eat. Contents may settle during shipping. Sold by weight, not volume.&lt;/div&gt;

Unfortunately, many protein supplements are blended with inferior sources of protein, such as low quality whey protein concentrate. These products often contain more lactose, which can cause gastrointestinal distress such as bloating, gas, and cramping.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eInferior sources of protein, gram for gram, are as not as pure as whey isolates. Whey protein isolate not only serves up more quality protein per scoop to ignite muscle protein synthesis, it’s also lower in unwanted lactose, fat, and carbohydrates than cheaper protein sources. It’s typically more expensive to manufacture, due to the advanced methods of processing it undergoes.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eWhey protein isolate is commonly processed two ways: ion exchange or micro\/ultrafiltration. To the unknowing buyer, you may think you’re getting the same thing but these two methods are not equal. The ion exchange process, used by many leading brands, selectively depletes several critical tiny molecules known as subfractions, which ultimately results in the denaturing (damaging) of the protein.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eThe whey protein in Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate has been filtered using the most advanced cross flow micro- and ultrafiltration technology to reduce fat, cholesterol, lactose and other unwanted components for an ultrapure, non-denatured isolate protein. The result is a top quality, rapid absorbing whey isolate that yields an ideal amino acid profile to fuel your body’s anabolic machinery.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"km-black\"\u003e\n\u003ch3 class=\"left-block-yellow\"\u003eWHY CHOOSE MICROPURE WHEY PROTEIN ISOLATE?\u003c\/h3\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eEach scoop of \u003cspan\u003eMicropure®\u003c\/span\u003e Whey Protein Isolate contains 25 grams of pure isolate – the highest quality and most bioavailable protein available. This ultra-premium whey protein isolate formula has an advanced, full-spectrum amino acid profile that includes EAAs, BCAAs, CAAs, and NAAs, to support increases in protein synthesis for serious muscle gains. Each scoop of Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate delivers:\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cmeta charset=\"utf-8\"\u003e\n\u003ch5 class=\"left-block-yellow\"\u003eEach scoop of MICROPURE Whey Protein Isolate delivers:\u003c\/h5\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"km-blackimage\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"\/\/cdn.shopify.com\/s\/files\/1\/1110\/3248\/files\/whey-2.jpg?v=1538045940\" alt=\"\"\u003e\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"km-lightgrey\"\u003e\n\u003ch3 class=\"left-block\"\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eTHE PROHYDROLASE ADVANTAGE\u003c\/strong\u003e \u003c\/h3\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eKaged Muscle researchers invested countless hours working to create a protein formula better than regular whey protein isolate. Infused with ProHydrolase® technology, the advanced Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate formula delivers.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eEach serving is supercharged with a precise 250 milligrams of ProHydrolase®, an innovative patented digestive (proteolytic) enzyme blend scientifically shown to be more effective for increasing protein digestion than whey protein on its own. Using this exclusive blend of enzymes the whey protein is rapidly hydrolyzed (broken down) in real-time, upon consumption, rather than during the manufacturing process using harsh chemicals. The result is an unrivaled whey protein isolate formula, scientifically designed to help boost digestion and absorption of its powerful muscle-building amino acids.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eWhey protein is a source of all nine essential amino acids.[1] To effectively promote muscle growth and strength, the protein must first be broken down into smaller, more usable protein fractions (i.e., di- and tri-peptides)[2] rapidly after consumption.[3] When whey protein is not broken down into its smallest fractions (common with cheaper, inferior sources of protein), the larger peptides can cause gastrointestinal discomfort such as bloating, gas, cramping for sensitive individuals. ProHydrolase® has been shown to promote more effective digestion of whey protein, promoting better absorption into the bloodstream.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eProHydrolase® rapidly breaks down the whey protein isolate into highly bioavailable micro fractions, allowing your body more easily absorb the protein and take full advantage of the available essential amino acids.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"km-darkgrey\"\u003e\n\u003ch3 class=\"left-block-yellow\"\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eULTRA-CLEAN FORMULA\u003c\/strong\u003e \u003c\/h3\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eLike all Kaged Muscle products, Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate has been scientifically formulated with only clean Micropure® ingredients, and it has been rigorously third-party tested and verified for purity, potency, and overall composition. Whey protein isolate, on the other hand, has 90% protein. Whey protein isolate goes through an advanced filtration process to reduce the amount of lactose, fat, and carbohydrates, ultimately yielding a purer, cleaner form of protein.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"faq-section\"\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eHow does Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate compare to Hydrolyzed Whey Protein?\u003c\/h4\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eThe difference between traditional forms of hydrolyzed whey protein and Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate is that our protein is hydrolyzed in real-time, at the time of consumption, thanks to the innovative ProHydrolase® Enzyme Technology. Proteins hydrolyzed during the manufacturing process are chemically treated to breakdown the protein into its smaller amino acid components, and the resulting material is then dried and packaged for your consumption.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eBecause Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate is rapidly hydrolyzed in real-time, we recommend you consume it within 15-20 minutes of mixing, or the product will start to taste bitter like hydrolyzed whey protein.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"faq-section\"\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eWhat should I look for on the label to identify a quality whey protein isolate?\u003c\/h4\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eMany brands use fancy buzzwords on their labels to disguise lower-quality protein sources contained within their products. If you want a high-quality whey protein powder, make sure whey protein isolate is the only source of protein listed in the ingredients. If the first or second ingredient is whey protein concentrate, then it’s time for a new protein powder.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cmeta charset=\"utf-8\"\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eCan I use Micropure Whey Protein Isolate if I am lactose intolerant?\u003c\/h4\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eA typical serving of Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate has less than 0.1 grams of lactose. Most experts agree that most individuals with lactose intolerance can safely consume this trace amount of lactose with no discomfort. Kaged Muscle’s Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate has been formulated to be everyone’s choice for the pure, clean, and fast digesting whey protein isolate on the market. With no amino spiking, protein blends or concentrates, and no added dyes or colors– bodybuilders and other athletes can support muscle recovery and boost gains in size and strength, without compromise.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cimg src=\"\/\/cdn.shopify.com\/s\/files\/1\/1110\/3248\/files\/Asset_2_4x_9a265541-08d3-4006-afea-892f8a95e07d.png?v=1538043637\" alt=\"\"\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"km-lightgrey\"\u003e\n\u003ch3 class=\"left-block\"\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eWHEY PROTEIN ISOLATE FOR SERIOUS GAINS\u003c\/strong\u003e \u003c\/h3\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eWith the vast amount of protein supplements on the market, it’s hard to know which ones are of the best quality and worth your hard-earned cash. Unfortunately, many protein supplements are blended with inferior sources of protein, such as low quality whey protein concentrate. These products often contain more lactose, which can cause gastrointestinal distress such as bloating, gas, and cramping.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eInferior sources of protein, gram for gram, are as not as pure as whey isolates. Whey protein isolate not only serves up more quality protein per scoop to ignite muscle protein synthesis, it’s also lower in unwanted lactose, fat, and carbohydrates than cheaper protein sources. It’s typically more expensive to manufacture, due to the advanced methods of processing it undergoes.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eWhey protein isolate is commonly processed two ways: ion exchange or micro\/ultrafiltration. To the unknowing buyer, you may think you’re getting the same thing but these two methods are not equal. The ion exchange process, used by many leading brands, selectively depletes several critical tiny molecules known as subfractions, which ultimately results in the denaturing (damaging) of the protein.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eThe whey protein in Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate has been filtered using the most advanced cross flow micro- and ultrafiltration technology to reduce fat, cholesterol, lactose and other unwanted components for an ultrapure, non-denatured isolate protein. The result is a top quality, rapid absorbing whey isolate that yields an ideal amino acid profile to fuel your body’s anabolic machinery.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"km-black\"\u003e\n\u003ch3 class=\"left-block-yellow\"\u003eWHY CHOOSE MICROPURE WHEY PROTEIN ISOLATE?\u003c\/h3\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eEach scoop of \u003cspan\u003eMicropure®\u003c\/span\u003e Whey Protein Isolate contains 25 grams of pure isolate – the highest quality and most bioavailable protein available. This ultra-premium whey protein isolate formula has an advanced, full-spectrum amino acid profile that includes EAAs, BCAAs, CAAs, and NAAs, to support increases in protein synthesis for serious muscle gains. Each scoop of Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate delivers:\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cmeta charset=\"utf-8\"\u003e\n\u003ch5 class=\"left-block-yellow\"\u003eEach scoop of MICROPURE Whey Protein Isolate delivers:\u003c\/h5\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"km-blackimage\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"\/\/cdn.shopify.com\/s\/files\/1\/1110\/3248\/files\/whey-2.jpg?v=1538045940\" alt=\"\"\u003e\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"km-lightgrey\"\u003e\n\u003ch3 class=\"left-block\"\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eTHE PROHYDROLASE ADVANTAGE\u003c\/strong\u003e \u003c\/h3\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eKaged Muscle researchers invested countless hours working to create a protein formula better than regular whey protein isolate. Infused with ProHydrolase® technology, the advanced Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate formula delivers.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eEach serving is supercharged with a precise 250 milligrams of ProHydrolase®, an innovative patented digestive (proteolytic) enzyme blend scientifically shown to be more effective for increasing protein digestion than whey protein on its own. Using this exclusive blend of enzymes the whey protein is rapidly hydrolyzed (broken down) in real-time, upon consumption, rather than during the manufacturing process using harsh chemicals. The result is an unrivaled whey protein isolate formula, scientifically designed to help boost digestion and absorption of its powerful muscle-building amino acids.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eWhey protein is a source of all nine essential amino acids.[1] To effectively promote muscle growth and strength, the protein must first be broken down into smaller, more usable protein fractions (i.e., di- and tri-peptides)[2] rapidly after consumption.[3] When whey protein is not broken down into its smallest fractions (common with cheaper, inferior sources of protein), the larger peptides can cause gastrointestinal discomfort such as bloating, gas, cramping for sensitive individuals. ProHydrolase® has been shown to promote more effective digestion of whey protein, promoting better absorption into the bloodstream.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eProHydrolase® rapidly breaks down the whey protein isolate into highly bioavailable micro fractions, allowing your body more easily absorb the protein and take full advantage of the available essential amino acids.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"km-darkgrey\"\u003e\n\u003ch3 class=\"left-block-yellow\"\u003e\n\u003cstrong\u003eULTRA-CLEAN FORMULA\u003c\/strong\u003e \u003c\/h3\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eLike all Kaged Muscle products, Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate has been scientifically formulated with only clean Micropure® ingredients, and it has been rigorously third-party tested and verified for purity, potency, and overall composition. We disclose every active ingredient in its full amount on the label—there’s nothing hidden. This clean formula is also designed with natural flavors, using an exclusive combination of ingredients for an unrivaled, great tasting protein anytime you desire a high-quality, high-protein drink.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"km-black\"\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"faq\"\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"faq-header\"\u003e\n\u003ch3 class=\"left-block-yellow\"\u003eFAQs\u003c\/h3\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"faq-section\"\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eWhat is the difference between Whey Protein Concentrate and Whey Protein Isolate?\u003c\/h4\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eWhey protein concentrate has only 80% protein and a higher amount of unwanted other material, such as lactose and ash, which can cause bloating and gas. Whey protein isolate, on the other hand, has 90% protein. Whey protein isolate goes through an advanced filtration process to reduce the amount of lactose, fat, and carbohydrates, ultimately yielding a purer, cleaner form of protein.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"faq-section\"\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eHow does Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate compare to Hydrolyzed Whey Protein?\u003c\/h4\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eThe difference between traditional forms of hydrolyzed whey protein and Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate is that our protein is hydrolyzed in real-time, at the time of consumption, thanks to the innovative ProHydrolase® Enzyme Technology. Proteins hydrolyzed during the manufacturing process are chemically treated to breakdown the protein into its smaller amino acid components, and the resulting material is then dried and packaged for your consumption.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eBecause Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate is rapidly hydrolyzed in real-time, we recommend you consume it within 15-20 minutes of mixing, or the product will start to taste bitter like hydrolyzed whey protein.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"faq-section\"\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eWhat should I look for on the label to identify a quality whey protein isolate?\u003c\/h4\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eMany brands use fancy buzzwords on their labels to disguise lower-quality protein sources contained within their products. If you want a high-quality whey protein powder, make sure whey protein isolate is the only source of protein listed in the ingredients. If the first or second ingredient is whey protein concentrate, then it’s time for a new protein powder.\u003c\/p\u003e\n\u003cmeta charset=\"utf-8\"\u003e\n\u003ch4\u003eCan I use Micropure Whey Protein Isolate if I am lactose intolerant?\u003c\/h4\u003e\n\u003cp class=\"p1\"\u003eA typical serving of Micropure® Whey Protein Isolate has less than 0.1 grams of lactose. Most experts agree that most individuals with lactose intolerance can safely consume this trace amount of lactose with no discomfort. &lt;strong&gt;Directions For CreaClear:&lt;/strong&gt; &lt;br&gt;As a dietary supplement, for the first 4 - 5 days (loading phase) mix one scoop with 8 -10 ounces of water or fruit juice (stir or shake vigorously for 20 - 30 seconds).
